    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<div id="review_293125630" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/293125630" />
    <a title="Angela Holtz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4646172-angela-holtz"><img alt="Angela Holtz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1313589673p2/4646172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/293125630?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela Holtz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela Holtz" href="/user/show/4646172-angela-holtz">Angela Holtz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/13347132-annabel-horton">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer293125630" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11426222658993768702">From <a href='http://lilacwolfandstuff.blogspot.com/2012/03/annabel-horton-lost-witch-of-salem.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lilac Wolf and Stuff</a><br/><br/>This book gave me chills. Following Annabel as she went from body to body, visited time periods past and future, and fought for lover and family over and over. This book is chocked full of action, magic and philosophy.<br/><br/>All through the book, though Annabel knows she is a witch, she also knows she is a Christian and that God has blessed her. She also spends a lot of time battling a demon who doesn't even have a bone to pick with her, it's a great aunt or something.<br/><br/>I will ad</span>
  <span id="freeText11426222658993768702" style="display:none">From <a href="http://lilacwolfandstuff.blogspot.com/2012/03/annabel-horton-lost-witch-of-salem.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Lilac Wolf and Stuff</a><br /><br />This book gave me chills. Following Annabel as she went from body to body, visited time periods past and future, and fought for lover and family over and over. This book is chocked full of action, magic and philosophy.<br /><br />All through the book, though Annabel knows she is a witch, she also knows she is a Christian and that God has blessed her. She also spends a lot of time battling a demon who doesn't even have a bone to pick with her, it's a great aunt or something.<br /><br />I will admit, while I adored this book I was uncomfortable with the idea that the only religions touched on were Christianity and Satanism (media's definition on that one, too). But that being said, it really did drive the story. There is such a stark disparity between God and Satan. It made the story so colorful.<br /><br />As for Annabel, she is not without sin. She stole the bodies of innocents early on. Then she only stole from those she deemed "evil" but I think the problem in that is thinking she has the right to judge. The other mistake is working so hard for revenge over the loss of money in the time period she keeps returning to.<br /><br />It's kind of weird. She goes all over, but there's a central progression to the story that anchors it. I liked all the characters - and truly there's not a complete hero among the bunch. Annabel has caused some of her own problems, and her children and grand children have caused others. It's not all on that demon.<br /><br />The story also has some harsh reality in it. It's very well written, with a polished and professional feel to it. Yeah! Seriously couldn't put this down. I worked so hard yesterday to clean the boys room and do the house work that needed to be done...but all I could think about was when it was time to stop and pick up that book again! So yup, this one is getting 5 stars. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11426222658993768702" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_264182190" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/264182190" />
    <a title="Delphina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7166602-delphina"><img alt="Delphina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1325691439p2/7166602.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/264182190?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Delphina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Delphina" href="/user/show/7166602-delphina">Delphina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/13347132-annabel-horton">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7166602-delphina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer264182190" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9843715874827970341">The story weaving in this book astonished me. I was really expecting the book to be very different than it was. I guess I had preconceived notions because I read so many para type books. This book, however, is unlike anything I have ever read. It was a cross between a family saga, historical fiction, horror and paranormal. That does not even do it justice, but it had elements from them all.<br/><br/>I loved how the author had "time travel" but did not allow themselves to get sucked into the normal time tr</span>
  <span id="freeText9843715874827970341" style="display:none">The story weaving in this book astonished me. I was really expecting the book to be very different than it was. I guess I had preconceived notions because I read so many para type books. This book, however, is unlike anything I have ever read. It was a cross between a family saga, historical fiction, horror and paranormal. That does not even do it justice, but it had elements from them all.<br /><br />I loved how the author had "time travel" but did not allow themselves to get sucked into the normal time travel traps. The way the characters moved through time allowed the story to really develop and to be reveled in a very intriguing way. I never really knew what was going to come next, but as a new scene developed you knew it made perfect sense.<br /><br />None of the characters were completely "good", which made the plot twists very interesting. They were flawed people, just like we are all flawed. There were times when I simply did not like some of the characters. I love it when read a book and actually care about the characters, even if it is in an "I can not believe you are doing this" kind of way.<br /><br />There is some true darkness in this book. There was the "evil" of the book, which you expect to be evil, but there was also some human darkness. You know children were being treated horribly during different parts of the book, but you never get in depth descriptions of it. This added to the horror of it. That being said, if this is an issue that is too difficult for you, this may not be the book for you.<br /><br />I am hoping that there will be a sequel to this book. I really would like to find out what happens next. <br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="9843715874827970341" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/257764543" />
    <a title="K J Bennett" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6799125-k-j-bennett"><img alt="K J Bennett" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1446674290p2/6799125.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/257764543?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K J Bennett" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K J Bennett" href="/user/show/6799125-k-j-bennett">K J Bennett</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/13347132-annabel-horton">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer257764543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14811096997674901155">Where do I start?<br/><br/>This novel is amazing: beautifully written, gripping, and un-putdownable (I nearly overran my journey to work via London Underground several times). <br/><br/>Vera Jane Cook has created a timeless character in Annabel Horton – literally. Destined for her soul to pass through time dimensions and to constantly face her demons, Annabel must save her extended family from the Devil’s clutches. When I say extended, I mean close relatives, extended by several hundred years!<br/><br/>Running at about 137,0</span>
  <span id="freeText14811096997674901155" style="display:none">Where do I start?<br /><br />This novel is amazing: beautifully written, gripping, and un-putdownable (I nearly overran my journey to work via London Underground several times). <br /><br />Vera Jane Cook has created a timeless character in Annabel Horton – literally. Destined for her soul to pass through time dimensions and to constantly face her demons, Annabel must save her extended family from the Devil’s clutches. When I say extended, I mean close relatives, extended by several hundred years!<br /><br />Running at about 137,000 words it is never tedious. It is, however, sometimes complex matter to keep up with the family tree, but it is well worth bearing with.<br /><br />At times heartfelt, always verging on the dramatic, Vera Jane Cook’s novel is a masterpiece. When reading this you may find yourself questioning time and reality, but I doubt you’ll question the abilities of this author. Five very large stars.<br /></span>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/27371034-annabel-horton-lost-witch-of-salem">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2842889381" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15091296553756209238"><strong>Brilliant!</strong><br/><br/>A hauntingly beautiful and well-written tale of the Lost Witch of Salem. I was mesmerized by the intriguing detail and uniqueness of this book. I've never read anything like it. <br/>The characters are so well defined and blend beautifully through time. The author weaves such intricacies throughout each time period and ties everything together in a jaw-dropping end. I hope for a sequel. I highly recommend this five-star book.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2825938683" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2825938683" />
    <a title="Suzanne Hare " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/88172371-suzanne-hare"><img alt="Suzanne Hare " src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2825938683?book_show_action=true">May 18, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne Hare " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne Hare " href="/user/show/88172371-suzanne-hare">Suzanne Hare </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/27371034-annabel-horton-lost-witch-of-salem">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2825938683" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer402756899621981193">This story is told by the main character, Patience Annabel Horton. Although it is named The Lost Witch of Salem, it is so very much more than a simple tale about a witch. The story begins with the events in her life leading up to her death. She believes she will be named as a witch because of her age and her beauty. She sees a spits who, although has no shape, she begins to love him. She receives mysterious love letters. Her fears are confirmed and she is accused of being a witch. She is hung an</span>
  <span id="freeText402756899621981193" style="display:none">This story is told by the main character, Patience Annabel Horton. Although it is named The Lost Witch of Salem, it is so very much more than a simple tale about a witch. The story begins with the events in her life leading up to her death. She believes she will be named as a witch because of her age and her beauty. She sees a spits who, although has no shape, she begins to love him. She receives mysterious love letters. Her fears are confirmed and she is accused of being a witch. She is hung and her spirt goes to a place of nothingness, she is alone and yet not alone. Sort of like how purgatory is described. After a while she can visit earth although no one can see or hear her. As time progresses she tries to enter a child’s body and takes over it, essentially bumping the soul of the child out. She lives within the child’s body until she dies at 29. I am going to stop there because you really need to read this book to get the overall experience.<br /><br />This is not just a novel, it is an experience. The story itself is long and complicated. The author expertly weaves the story through time and dimensions. While the story is linear for Annabel, time is not. This a complex story dealing with human nature, our weakness and strengths, good and evil, the devil and god. The characters are well devolved and all of are flawed yet some have Redeeming qualities. It is an emotional rollercoaster. The places, scenes and characters are described in great detail. The subject matter is at time uncomfortable to read. This is a book that can be read at many different levels and the reader can glean what they want out of it. I know this book had a profound effect on me as a reader. Did I enjoy the book? I am not sure, it is one of those great reads that take time to appreciate. Did I find the book compelling? Yes. Did I feel comfortable reading it? No, this books deals with uncomfortable aspects of human nature within a religious context. I had to stop reading several times to fully absorb it. As a reader it pushed my limits. Would I read it again? Yes, I believe I will. Some books spark a change in how you view things, this is one of them. <br /><br />Keep in mind, this is a long book, very complex in nature and not for teenagers. Should you read it? Yes, it is an amazing work of art written by an extremely talent author. It is a gem.<br /><br />I received a free copy of this book via Booksprout and am voluntarily leaving a review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="402756899621981193" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

The devil has sent one of this minions, Urban Grandier to force her to use her abilities to keep her family safe throughout time. Annabel does Urban’s bidding while she tries to figure out why her and her family. Annabel is determined to keep her family safe throughout time but it’s </span>
  <span id="freeText13975890152015996761" style="display:none">Annabel is a Christian woman that has been blessed with some special abilities. The devil has sent one of this minions, Urban Grandier to force her to use her abilities to keep her family safe throughout time. Annabel does Urban’s bidding while she tries to figure out why her and her family. There has to be a reason and way out of the torment her and her family go through.<br /> <br />This story starts out slow but takes of like a shot. Annabel is determined to keep her family safe throughout time but it’s not always his fault the troubles they find themselves in, they make plenty of errors on their own too. I really like how Annabel travels through time. She may be stealing bodies but there are no time travel paradoxes that she runs into.<br /><br />This is a really good story and worth checking out. The writing is very detailed and makes you feel the scenes. I will admit that I did get irritated with some of it since it drew out paragraphs without really tell you what was going on. It is definitely a different approach to paranormal stories.<br /><br />I received a complimentary copy of this book. I voluntarily chose to read and post an honest review.<br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Valery" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Valery" href="/user/show/4013735-valery">Valery</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2811401511" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7093361013022130248">Annabel Horton: Lost Witch of Salem by Olivia Hardy Ray is a heady mix of time travel, witches, ghosts, and the devil. As the lost witch of Salem, Annabel must fight for her family from demons and the devil himself. From a time travel perspective this is certainly a unique book, one that fits well within the confines of witch trials in Salem. Of course the horrific hangings lend an eerie atmosphere to the book. The writing is some of the most detailed you will ever read, putting one in mind of m</span>
  <span id="freeText7093361013022130248" style="display:none">Annabel Horton: Lost Witch of Salem by Olivia Hardy Ray is a heady mix of time travel, witches, ghosts, and the devil. As the lost witch of Salem, Annabel must fight for her family from demons and the devil himself. From a time travel perspective this is certainly a unique book, one that fits well within the confines of witch trials in Salem. Of course the horrific hangings lend an eerie atmosphere to the book. The writing is some of the most detailed you will ever read, putting one in mind of much older literary works. Sometimes this seems a little overdone in spots, as one struggles to follow the story line, there is so much descriptive detail. However, ultimately that doesn't detract from the overarching theme or plot of the story. A touch of hopeful romance with a ghost, time travel, and creepy happenings figure prominently in the book, giving it a unique and well rounded feel. Overall, an interesting and engaging book that you will enjoy if for nothing more than the historical aspect of the witch trials. Highly recommend. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7093361013022130248" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2824123628" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2824123628" />
    <a title="Jamie Jack" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/87796500-jamie-jack"><img alt="Jamie Jack" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1566896230p2/87796500.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2824123628?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie Jack" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie Jack" href="/user/show/87796500-jamie-jack">Jamie Jack</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/27371034-annabel-horton-lost-witch-of-salem">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87796500-jamie-jack?shelf=p-2019">p-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87796500-jamie-jack?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2824123628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14105406412963761505">At the start of the book, Annabel tells us that she is going to portray the real history of what happened at Salem at the time of the witch trials. She goes on to do much more, revealing a little of her life as a human the first time around and as a spirit who occasionally returns to a living human being. The book is full of time travel, some violence, demons and devils, and—of course—witches.<br/><br/>The author did a good job weaving the story in and out of time in such a way that you didn’t feel lost. </span>
  <span id="freeText14105406412963761505" style="display:none">At the start of the book, Annabel tells us that she is going to portray the real history of what happened at Salem at the time of the witch trials. She goes on to do much more, revealing a little of her life as a human the first time around and as a spirit who occasionally returns to a living human being. The book is full of time travel, some violence, demons and devils, and—of course—witches.<br /><br />The author did a good job weaving the story in and out of time in such a way that you didn’t feel lost. The narrator, despite being involved in the incidents recounted, seemed to be recounting from a distance, so much of the story felt like it was told rather than shown. I found that a little off-putting because it creates distance between the reader and the story. Some other reviewers have mentioned the language seems a little old fashioned; perhaps just a little, but I think that the narrative distance makes it seem more so that than it actually is.<br /><br />I received a free copy of this book, but that did not affect my review.<br /><br />Read my other reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.readingfanaticreviews.com">https://www.readingfanaticreviews.com</a>.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2812704724" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17045624202261761153">This work of fiction is one of the most versatile stories I have read for quite some time, thanks to its many dimensions. The book makes you wish for the sequel as it takes you on a trip in these dimensions with a healthy mix of time travel, the devil, ghosts, and witches. The horrific hanging gives the book an eerie atmosphere.<br/><br/>Cook has managed to produce some of the most detailed writings I have ever read, but some sections sound as if they have been overdone. The plot and the overarching theme</span>
  <span id="freeText17045624202261761153" style="display:none">This work of fiction is one of the most versatile stories I have read for quite some time, thanks to its many dimensions. The book makes you wish for the sequel as it takes you on a trip in these dimensions with a healthy mix of time travel, the devil, ghosts, and witches. The horrific hanging gives the book an eerie atmosphere.<br /><br />Cook has managed to produce some of the most detailed writings I have ever read, but some sections sound as if they have been overdone. The plot and the overarching theme of the book have been developed carefully, though, and the touch of romance is a good distraction from the chilling atmosphere. Too much detail may make you struggle to follow the story in some parts, but overall, the book will entertain you because of the creative story.<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668538167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8242993209648147894">I received this book free from First Reads in exchange for a honest review.<br/><br/>The book is not what I thought it would be. When I got it, I was pleased to see it wasn't the typical "Salem Witch" book. However, I STRUGGLED to read this book. I about quit several times, but kept on reading. I finally stopped about chapter 36. I can't do it anymore, and I rarely set aside a book.<br/><br/>This book had great possibilities...but never lived up to any of them. The whole time travel thing got to be old, fast. The b</span>
  <span id="freeText8242993209648147894" style="display:none">I received this book free from First Reads in exchange for a honest review.<br /><br />The book is not what I thought it would be. When I got it, I was pleased to see it wasn't the typical "Salem Witch" book. However, I STRUGGLED to read this book. I about quit several times, but kept on reading. I finally stopped about chapter 36. I can't do it anymore, and I rarely set aside a book.<br /><br />This book had great possibilities...but never lived up to any of them. The whole time travel thing got to be old, fast. The book never goes anywhere, just a lot of the same thing over and over. New identity/same problems/new problems that make no sense to the story/no resolution/repeat until I couldn't take it anymore. I can't keep any of the characters straight at this point, and if there is a plot, I can not for the life of me figure out what it is. Way too much flipping time periods and trying to remember/figure out who/where people are, then they add more people to make it even worse. For such a powerful witch, Annabel seems to be pretty clueless and unable to control her powers or avoid the bad things that happen one after another.<br /><br />Sorry. Not for me. I thought this would be so much better, and parts of it were ok, but that's all. <br /><br />I WISH my favorite line in the book were true. "There are secrets in my tale worth knowing". </span>
  <a data-text-id="8242993209648147894" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1054275641" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1054275641" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4885159-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296157092p2/4885159.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1054275641?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/4885159-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1054275641" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6044543623245455667">Unlike anything else I have ever read, this story is a mix of historical fiction, time travel and body hopping, prejudice (against both color and sexual preferences,) culture and beliefs in various eras, and is a complicated family saga. For geneologists this is both a dream and a nightmare. Don't go looking for family loyalty.<br/><br/>As with many tales of the Salem Witch times, it is good vs evil and questioning the existance of God and or Devil.<br/>The book is full of beautifully descriptive passages. Dur</span>
  <span id="freeText6044543623245455667" style="display:none">Unlike anything else I have ever read, this story is a mix of historical fiction, time travel and body hopping, prejudice (against both color and sexual preferences,) culture and beliefs in various eras, and is a complicated family saga. For geneologists this is both a dream and a nightmare. Don't go looking for family loyalty.<br /><br />As with many tales of the Salem Witch times, it is good vs evil and questioning the existance of God and or Devil.<br />The book is full of beautifully descriptive passages. During various forms of existance, time does not pass at the same pace. Lies and deceit abound and sometimes you are not sure who to trust. <br />Annabel is very strong and true. As often as evil tries to lure (or force) her into the shadows, her soul prevails.<br />She also has a playful and mischevious nature. A well rounded and developed character.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6044543623245455667" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer257032656" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17225556311804276815">3 and 3/4 stars for me.<br/><br/>Annabel Horton is cursed. This story, written in the style of classical literature, describes Annabel's journey through the dimensions of time trying to reunite with her loved ones and fight the evil force that is torturing them all. <br/><br/>The book has an adult content warning up front which is quite warranted. This was a very different type of book for me - much darker than I usually read. Although dark, it is not overly graphic which I appreciate. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('igNzcXY1GmaKYHo2DiFJaEZBcxxn5vYoyPlveLIhkBOwJRqjzWvTDi1Lzlf51EO3kB6U1KlreE+ThynJf2JiiQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ab7fA8MZh1XzIUQaAIJXVPSAIlTudu/kJWMHORnp7tM7mLbReEdOPVQK8Hv3d12LIt/FnCD7YYN+HUGI1KocSQ==')})
  }

It is a Pandoras box of emotions, situations, opportunities, and failures, all wrapped into a package we call life. Nobody is immune, but everyone has the opportunity to grow tall or wither like a flower in harsh light. Its completely up to us how we choose to respond. Finding Hope in the Darkness of Grief is a gleaning of insights from artist Diamante Lavender. For her, life has been a long, difficult road, but it has taught many poignant lessons. Her poetry collection is an exploration of the human soul, a traversing of situations that life throws at us. Diamante has always been intrigued by the ability to overcome and move on to bigger and better things. She writes to encourage hope and possibility in those who read her stories. If she can help others heal, as she has, then Diamantes work as an author and artist will have been well spent. She believes that everyone should try to leave a positive mark on the world, to make it a better place for all. Writing is the way that she is attempting to leave her markone story at a time.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"12485220051400402723\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return Above al<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText8966472401729449903\" style=\"display:none\">From the Foreword by Marian Wright EdelmanAfrica’s Child is an unforgettable and searingly personal book….In the face of repeated obstacles and injustices, Nhambu continued to analyze the world around her with wit and a sharp sense of humor. Above all, as a very young child she decided one day that even if there was no other person in the world who loved and wanted her, she was going to love and care for herself—and that decision changed the course of her life. Africa’s Child is the story of a mixed-race girl growing up in the Usambara Mountains of Tanzania, East Africa. Raised in an orphanage with no knowledge of her origins or family, she endured abandonment, hardships, severe illnesses, and bullying. Her experiences as a child and teenager included physical, emotional, and sexual abuse, social stigma, and racial discrimination.Yet Nhambu tells her inspiring story with warmth and humor. Her questioning mind probes the African tribal realities and multi-cultural complexities that impacted her life both at the orphanage and schools run by German nuns as well as at an African high school with American nuns. Nhambu not only survived her childhood but triumphed. Her faith and resilience, along with a belief in learning and her tenacious pursuit of an education, sustained her through many challenges. Dance, especially African tribal dance, became the way she healed and nourished her spirit. Through the love and commitment of an American teacher she met in Africa, Nhambu was able to pursue her dream of education and a new life for herself. The first book in her three-part memoir ends as she is leaving Africa for university studies in America on a full scholarship.Maria Nhambu is the creator of Aerobics With Soul®, a fitness workout
